2026-05-01T05:39:19.5715253Z ##[group]Run # Note: There is currently no way to distinguish between undefined variables and empty strings in GitHub Actions.
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5716476Z [36;1m# Note: There is currently no way to distinguish between undefined variables and empty strings in GitHub Actions.[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5717404Z [36;1m# This limitation affects how we handle default values and empty inputs.[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5718127Z [36;1m# For more information, see: https://github.com/actions/runner/issues/924[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5718531Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5718912Z [36;1m# The following logic implements the configuration priority described in the README:[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5719334Z [36;1m#[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5719509Z [36;1m# Inputs[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5719714Z [36;1m# Environment Variables[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5719957Z [36;1m# Config File[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5720162Z [36;1m# Defaults[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5720369Z [36;1m#[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5720769Z [36;1m# As noted above defaults are awkward to handle as GitHub Actions will inject those values as the input[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5721450Z [36;1m# if the caller doesn't provide them, thus if the input matches the default we don't set it as we[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5722123Z [36;1m# can't tell the difference.  Plus if we did set it when it was the default value then it could potentially[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5722862Z [36;1m# override an external environment variable, or something in the callers configuration file, which then wouldn't[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5723458Z [36;1m# match the configuration priority that is documented.[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5723795Z [36;1mset_env_var_if_provided() {[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5724048Z [36;1m  local var_name="$1"[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5724506Z [36;1m  local input_value="$2"[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5724774Z [36;1m  local default_value="$3"[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5725017Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5725311Z [36;1m  if [ -n "$input_value" ] && [ "$input_value" != "$default_value" ]; then[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5725801Z [36;1m    # If action was provided with explicit input by the caller set that[0m

2026-05-01T05:39:19.5727191Z [36;1m  fi[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5727366Z [36;1m}[0m
2026-05-01T05:39:19.5727535Z [36;1m[0m

2026-05-01T05:40:54.6652350Z ##[warning]Node.js 20 actions are deprecated. The following actions are running on Node.js 20 and may not work as expected: actions/checkout@v4, docker/build-push-action@v5, docker/setup-buildx-action@v3, docker/setup-qemu-action@v3, github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v3. Actions will be forced to run with Node.js 24 by default starting June 2nd, 2026. Node.js 20 will be removed from the runner on September 16th, 2026. Please check if updated versions of these actions are available that support Node.js 24. To opt into Node.js 24 now, set the FORCE_JAVASCRIPT_ACTIONS_TO_NODE24=true environment variable on the runner or in your workflow file. Once Node.js 24 becomes the default, you can temporarily opt out by setting ACTIONS_ALLOW_USE_UNSECURE_NODE_VERSION=true. For more information see: https://github.blog/changelog/2025-09-19-deprecation-of-node-20-on-github-actions-runners/
